* Word Tree / Roget's Thesaurus


﻿* Class I. Words Expressing Abstract Relations

** Section I. Existence

*** 1. Being, in The Abstract

***** existence 1

 + abide    v.容忍，忍受    [a-bide]
 + absolute    a.绝对的，完全的; 无(条件)限制的    [ab-so-lute]
 + authentic    a.真正的；法律证实的    [au-then-tic]
 + endure    v.忍受，忍耐    [en-dure]
 + entity    n.实体，统一体    [en-ti-ty]
 + essential    a.本质的；n.要素，实质    [es-sen-tial]
 + extant    a.现存的，传世的    [ex-tant]
 + prevail    v.战胜；盛行    [pre-vail]
 + subsistence    n.生存，生计；存在    [sub-sist-ence]
 + substantial    a.坚固的，结实的；实质的    [sub-stan-tial]
 + substantive    a.根本的；独立存在的    [sub-stan-tive]

 + extinct    a.绝种的，不存在的    [ex-tinct]
 + extinction    n.熄灭；消灭    [ex-tinc-tion]
 + extirpation    n.根除，铲除    [ex-tir-pa-tion]
 + insubstantial    a.非实体的；薄弱的    [in-sub-stan-tial]
 + nil    n.无，零    [nil]
 + nonentity    n.不重要之人或事    [non-en-ti-ty]
 + nullify    v.使无效，取消    [nul-li-fy]
 + obliterate    v.涂掉，擦掉    [o-blit-e-rate]
 + perish    v.死，暴卒    [per-ish]
 + potential    a.潜在的，有可能性的    [po-ten-tial]
 + remove    v.移走；脱掉；迁移    [re-move]
 + spectral    a.幽灵的    [spec-tral]
 + vain    a.自负的；徒劳的    [vain]
 + virtual    a.实质上的，实际上的    [vir-tu-al]
 + visionary    a.有远见的；幻想的；n.空想家    [vi-sion-ar-y]

 + conservative    a.保守的，守旧的    [con-serv-a-tive]

* Class III. Words Relating to Matter

** Section I. Matter in General

***** materiality 316

 - corporeal    a.肉体的，身体的；物质的    [cor-po-re-al]
 - objective    a.客观的；n.目标    [ob-jec-tive]
 + palpable    a.可触知的，明显的    [pal-pa-ble]
 + ponderable    a.可估量的    [pon-der-a-ble]
 - principle    n.原则，原理；道德准则    [prin-ci-ple]
 + sensible    a.明智的；可感觉到的    [sen-si-ble]
 + somatic    a.肉体的    [so-mat-ic]
 - substance    n.大意，根据，实质；物质    [sub-stance]
 - substantial    a.坚固的，结实的；实质的    [sub-stan-tial]
 - tangible    a.可触摸的    [tan-gi-ble]

***** immateriality 317

 + disembodied    a.无实体的，空洞的    [dis-em-bod-ied]
 - incorporate    v.合并，并入    [in-cor-po-rate]
 + spiritual    a.精神的    [spir-it-u-al]
 - subjective    a.主观的，想象的    [sub-jec-tive]
 + unearthly    a.奇异的    [un-earth-ly]

***** world 318

 + celestial    a.天体的，天上的    [ce-les-ti-al]

** Section IV. Antagonism

*** 1. Conditional Antagonism

***** difficulty 704

 - awkward    a.笨拙的；难用的；不便的    [awk-ward]

*** 2. Active Antagonism

***** hindrance 706

 + avert    v.避免，防止    [a-vert]
 - balk    n.大方木料；v.妨碍；(因困难等)不愿前进或从事某事    [balk]
 - bar    v.禁止，阻挡；n.条，棒    [ba-r]
 - barricade    v.设栅阻挡；n.栅栏    [bar-ri-cade]
 - barrier    n.路障；障碍    [bar-ri-er]
 - blockade    v./n.封锁    [block-ade]
 - bolt    v.急逃(to dash out; dart)；螺栓，门栓    [bolt]
 - boom    n.繁荣昌盛时期；v.发出深沉有回响的声音    [boom]
 - check    v.使突然停止，阻止    [check]
 - choke    v.(使)窒息，阻塞    [choke]
 - circumvent    v.回避；用计谋战胜或规避    [cir-cum-vent]
 - clog    n.障碍; v.阻塞    [clog]
 - contravene    v.违背(法规，习俗等)    [con-tra-vene]
 - counteract    v.消除，抵消    [coun-ter-act]
 - cramp    n.铁箍，夹子；v.把…箍紧    [cramp]

 + aristocracy    n.贵族；贵族政府，贵族统治    [ar-is-toc-ra-cy]

*** 3. Interchange of Property

***** barter 794
